is one of the most played board games in the world, play with your friends, try to defeat your opponents with strategy, reasoning and a little bit of luck.\r\nGeneral rules of dominoes:\r\n- Blocking game\r\nThe most basic dominos variant is for two players and requires a double six set. The 28 domino tiles are shuffled face down and form the stock or boneyard. Each player draws seven tiles; the remainder are not used. Once the players begin drawing tiles, they are typically placed on-edge before the players, so that each player can see his own domino tiles, but none can see the value of other players' tiles. Every player can thus see how many tiles remain in the other players' hands at all times during gameplay. One player begins by downing (playing the first tile) one of their tiles. In different games first tiles are also different. In Muggins player should start with the highest double (6-6), in Bergen the first move should be 0-0, in Mexican train each round starts with the next lower double. This tile starts the line of play, a series of tiles in which adjacent tiles touch with matching, i.e. equal, values. The players alternately extend the line of play with one tile at one of its two ends. The game ends when one player wins by playing their last tile, or when the game is blocked because neither player can play. If that occurs, whoever caused the block gets all of the remaining player points not counting their own.\r\n- Scoring game\r\nPlayers accrue points during game play for certain configurations, moves, or emptying one's hand. Most scoring games use variations of the draw game. In Muggins (All fives) player must make the open ends of the layout add up to 5s or a multiple of five (5s, 10, 15, 20, etc.) In bergen player scores when numbers on the open ends are equal. If a player does not call \"domino\" before the tile is laid on the table, and another player says 'domino' after the tile is laid, the first player must pick up an extra domino. In Mexican train the double zero domino is scored as 50 points.\r\n- Draw game\r\nIn a draw game (blocking or scoring), players are additionally allowed to draw as many tiles as desired from the stock before playing a tile. The score of a game is the number of pips in the losing player's hand plus the number of pips in the stock. Most rules prescribe that two tiles need to remain in the stock. The Draw game is often referred to as simply \"dominos\".\r\n\r\nIf you like board games like Checkers, Mahjong, Backgammon and Chess, you will love Dominoes: Best Classic Dominoes Board Game.","ProductFamilyName":"Games","Schema":"Card;1"},{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V8.One.CardModel, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ProductId":"9NWSPGNK6X3G","TileLayout":"Poster","Title":"Extreme Car Stunts Racing","Images":[{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V2.ImageItem, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ImageType":"tile","Url":"http://store-images.s-microsoft.com/image/apps.35550.14438838544424031.542d6d68-fe0f-4da7-930a-99b50389175a.da760ea9-a28f-434d-95b1-f637007e0864","Height":300,"Width":300,"BackgroundColor":"#ffffff","ForegroundColor":"","Caption":"","ImagePositionInfo":""},{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V2.ImageItem, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ImageType":"tile","Url":"http://store-images.s-microsoft.com/image/apps.38307.14438838544424031.542d6d68-fe0f-4da7-930a-99b50389175a.fcb99f41-bf3f-4267-91b3-5918cb2aa3b9","Height":300,"Width":620,"BackgroundColor":"#ffffff","ForegroundColor":"","Caption":"","ImagePositionInfo":""}],"DisplayPrice":"Kostenlos","Price":0.0,"AverageRating":5.0,"RatingsCount":"1","PackageFamilyNames":["57673GlobalEntertainment.ExtremeCarStuntsRacing_jysam6mhz54mr"],"ContentIds":["b807abfe-56ca-32ea-97cf-69dfc38e3e3d"],"GamingOptionsXboxLive":false,"AvailableDevicesDisplayText":"","AvailableDevicesNarratorText":"PC","TypeTag":"app","RecommendationReason":"","LongDescription":"Extreme Car Stunts is the best car simulator with 3D graphics and realistic physics! Eine einfache Bedienungsoberfläche und Sprachtipps ermöglichen sogar dem kleinsten Kind mit den Bildern selbstständig zu spielen.\r\nAus Erfahrung wissen wir, dass Kinder sehr gerne eine Serie von farbenfrohen Bilder mit Musik ansehen und sie werden Sie danach fragen die Bilder immer wieder zu sehen. Gemäß Glenn Doman, einem amerikanischen Physiotherapeut und Gründer des “The Institutes for the Achievement of Human Potential”-Institutes, hilft das teilnehmen in dieser Art von pädagogischen Aktivitäten (für 5-10 Minuten pro Tag) der Reizung zahlreicher Bereiche des Gehirnes. Demzufolge wird das fotografische Gedächtnis des Kindes geformt, das Kind entwickelt sich schneller als andere Gleichaltrige und das Kind erhält, beginnend in der frühen Kindheit, Zugang zu einer Welt von umfassendem Wissen.\r\n\r\nDie Hauptsache, in der Doman vollkommen richtig liegt, ist, dass je jünger ein Kind ist, desto einfach kann er oder sie Wissen aufnehmen. Es ist wichtig diese Fähigkeit zu nutzen, solange sie verfügbar ist.\r\n\r\nDie Anwendung kann als Unterstützungsbeihilfe in dem Erlernen von Fremdsprachen verwendet werden.
